## Section 1: Flask Routes Specification (Backend)

| Route Path               | Function Name            | HTTP Method | Template Rendered         | Context Variables Passed                                                                              |
|--------------------------|--------------------------|-------------|---------------------------|-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| /                        | root_redirect            | GET         | Redirect to `/dashboard`  | None                                                                                                |
| /dashboard               | dashboard_view           | GET         | dashboard.html            | featured_auctions: list of dict{auction_id: int, item_name: str, current_bid: float},
|                          |                          |             |                           | trending_auctions: list of dict{auction_id: int, item_name: str, current_bid: float, bid_count: int},
|                          |                          |             |                           | (additional navigation elements no context needed)                                                |
| /catalog                 | auction_catalog          | GET         | catalog.html              | auctions: list of dict{
|                          |                          |             |                           | auction_id: int, item_name: str, description: str, category: str, current_bid: float, end_time: str (datetime in str), image_url: str
|                          |                          |             |                           | },
|                          |                          |             |                           | categories: list of dict{category_id: int, category_name: str} (for category filter options)         |
| /auction/<int:auction_id>| auction_details          | GET         | auction_details.html      | auction: dict{
|                          |                          |             |                           | auction_id: int, item_name: str, description: str, current_bid: float, end_time: str, status: str
|                          |                          |             |                           | },
|                          |                          |             |                           | bid_history: list of dict{bidder_name: str, bid_amount: float, bid_timestamp: str}                    |
| /auction/<int:auction_id>/place_bid | place_bid           | GET         | place_bid.html            | auction: dict{auction_id: int, item_name: str, minimum_bid: float}                                  |
| /auction/<int:auction_id>/place_bid | submit_bid          | POST        | place_bid.html            | auction: dict{auction_id: int, item_name: str, minimum_bid: float}, error_message: str (optional)     |
| /bids                    | bid_history_view         | GET         | bid_history.html          | bids: list of dict{
|                          |                          |             |                           | bid_id: int, auction_name: str, bidder_name: str, bid_amount: float, bid_timestamp: str
|                          |                          |             |                           | },
|                          |                          |             |                           | auctions: list of dict{auction_id: int, auction_name: str} (for filter dropdown)                      |
| /categories              | categories_view          | GET         | categories.html           | categories: list of dict{category_id: int, category_name: str, description: str, item_count: int}     |
| /winners                 | winners_view             | GET         | winners.html              | winners: list of dict{auction_id: int, item_name: str, winner_name: str, winning_bid: float}          |
| /trending                | trending_auctions_view   | GET         | trending.html             | trending_auctions: list of dict{
|                          |                          |             |                           | auction_id: int, item_name: str, bid_count: int, current_bid: float, trending_rank: int, time_period: str

  - browse-auctions-button: url_for('auction_catalog')
  - view-bids-button: url_for('bid_history_view')
  - trending-auctions-button: url_for('trending_auctions_view')

## Section 3: Data File Schemas (Backend)

### 1. Auctions Data
- Path: data/auctions.txt
- Format: Pipe-delimited (|), no header line
- Fields:
  1. auction_id (int)
  2. item_name (str)
  3. description (str)
  4. category (str)
  5. starting_bid (float)
  6. current_bid (float)
  7. end_time (str: "YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM")
  8. status (str: "Active", "Closed", etc.)
  9. image_url (str)
- Purpose: Stores all auction items with details and current bidding status.
- Examples:
  - 1|Vintage Leather Watch|Antique leather wristwatch from the 1950s|Collectibles|25.00|45.50|2025-02-15 18:00|Active|watch.jpg
  - 2|iPhone 14 Pro|Latest Apple smartphone in excellent condition|Electronics|500.00|620.00|2025-02-10 12:00|Active|iphone.jpg
  - 3|Wooden Desk|Beautiful oak wood desk with original finish|Furniture|75.00|110.00|2025-02-08 20:00|Closed|desk.jpg

---

### 2. Categories Data
- Path: data/categories.txt
- Format: Pipe-delimited (|), no header line
- Fields:
  1. category_id (int)
  2. category_name (str)
  3. description (str)
  4. item_count (int)
- Purpose: Contains all auction categories with descriptions and counts.
- Examples:
  - 1|Electronics|Digital devices and gadgets|15
  - 2|Collectibles|Rare and valuable collector items|28
  - 3|Furniture|Household furniture and decor|12

---

### 3. Bids Data
- Path: data/bids.txt
- Format: Pipe-delimited (|), no header line
- Fields:
  1. bid_id (int)
  2. auction_id (int)
  3. bidder_name (str)
  4. bid_amount (float)
  5. bid_timestamp (str: "YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM")
- Purpose: Records all bids placed with details.
- Examples:
  - 1|1|Alice Johnson|45.50|2025-02-05 14:30
  - 2|2|Bob Williams|620.00|2025-02-05 15:45
  - 3|3|Charlie Brown|110.00|2025-02-04 10:15

---

### 4. Winners Data
- Path: data/winners.txt
- Format: Pipe-delimited (|), no header line
- Fields:
  1. winner_id (int)
  2. auction_id (int)
  3. item_name (str)
  4. winner_name (str)
  5. winning_bid (float)
  6. win_date (str: "YYYY-MM-DD")
- Purpose: Lists auction winning items with winner details.
- Examples:
  - 1|3|Wooden Desk|Charlie Brown|110.00|2025-02-08
  - 2|5|Victorian Mirror|Diana Prince|95.00|2025-02-03
  - 3|7|Vintage Books Set|Eve Stewart|150.00|2025-02-01

---

### 5. Bid History Data
- Path: data/bid_history.txt
- Format: Pipe-delimited (|), no header line
- Fields:
  1. history_id (int)
  2. auction_id (int)
  3. auction_name (str)
  4. bidder_name (str)
  5. bid_amount (float)
  6. bid_timestamp (str: "YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM")
- Purpose: Tracks all bid events historically.
- Examples:
  - 1|1|Vintage Leather Watch|Alice Johnson|40.00|2025-02-05 13:00
  - 2|1|Vintage Leather Watch|Frank Miller|42.50|2025-02-05 13:45
  - 3|2|iPhone 14 Pro|Bob Williams|620.00|2025-02-05 15:45

---

### 6. Items Data
- Path: data/items.txt
- Format: Pipe-delimited (|), no header line
- Fields:
  1. item_id (int)
  2. auction_id (int)
  3. item_name (str)
  4. starting_price (float)
  5. category (str)
  6. condition (str)
  7. seller_name (str)
- Purpose: Stores detailed item information associated with auctions.
- Examples:
  - 1|1|Vintage Leather Watch|25.00|Collectibles|Excellent|John Collector
  - 2|2|iPhone 14 Pro|500.00|Electronics|Like New|Tech Store
  - 3|3|Wooden Desk|75.00|Furniture|Good|Antique Shop

---

### 7. Trending Data
- Path: data/trending.txt
- Format: Pipe-delimited (|), no header line
- Fields:
  1. auction_id (int)
  2. item_name (str)
  3. bid_count (int)
  4. current_bid (float)
  5. trending_rank (int)
  6. time_period (str: e.g. "This Week")
- Purpose: Contains ranked trending auction information.
- Examples:
  - 2|iPhone 14 Pro|12|620.00|1|This Week
  - 1|Vintage Leather Watch|8|45.50|2|This Week
  - 5|Vintage Camera|6|85.00|3|This Week

---

# End of Design Specification Document


=== app.py ===
from flask import Flask, render_template, redirect, url_for, request
import os
from datetime import datetime

app = Flask(__name__)
app.config['SECRET_KEY'] = 'dev-secret-key'

data_dir = 'data'

# Utility functions to load data

def load_auctions():
    auctions = []
    path = os.path.join(data_dir, 'auctions.txt')
    if os.path.exists(path):
        with open(path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
            for line in f:
                parts = line.strip().split('|')
                if len(parts) == 9:
                    auctions.append({
                        'auction_id': int(parts[0]),
                        'item_name': parts[1],
                        'description': parts[2],
                        'category': parts[3],
                        'starting_bid': float(parts[4]),
                        'current_bid': float(parts[5]),
                        'end_time': parts[6],
                        'status': parts[7],
                        'image_url': parts[8]
                    })
    return auctions


def load_categories():
    categories = []
    path = os.path.join(data_dir, 'categories.txt')
    if os.path.exists(path):
        with open(path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
            for line in f:
                parts = line.strip().split('|')
                if len(parts) == 4:
                    categories.append({
                        'category_id': int(parts[0]),
                        'category_name': parts[1],
                        'description': parts[2],
                        'item_count': int(parts[3])
                    })
    return categories


def load_bids():
    bids = []
    path = os.path.join(data_dir, 'bids.txt')
    if os.path.exists(path):
        with open(path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
            for line in f:
                parts = line.strip().split('|')
                if len(parts) == 5:
                    bids.append({
                        'bid_id': int(parts[0]),
                        'auction_id': int(parts[1]),
                        'bidder_name': parts[2],
                        'bid_amount': float(parts[3]),
                        'bid_timestamp': parts[4]
                    })
    return bids


def load_winners():
    winners = []
    path = os.path.join(data_dir, 'winners.txt')
    if os.path.exists(path):
        with open(path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
            for line in f:
                parts = line.strip().split('|')
                if len(parts) == 6:
                    winners.append({
                        'winner_id': int(parts[0]),
                        'auction_id': int(parts[1]),
                        'item_name': parts[2],
                        'winner_name': parts[3],
                        'winning_bid': float(parts[4]),
                        'win_date': parts[5]
                    })
    return winners


def load_bid_history():
    bid_history = []
    path = os.path.join(data_dir, 'bid_history.txt')
    if os.path.exists(path):
        with open(path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
            for line in f:
                parts = line.strip().split('|')
                if len(parts) == 6:
                    bid_history.append({
                        'history_id': int(parts[0]),
                        'auction_id': int(parts[1]),
                        'auction_name': parts[2],
                        'bidder_name': parts[3],
                        'bid_amount': float(parts[4]),
                        'bid_timestamp': parts[5]
                    })
    return bid_history


def load_trending():
    trending = []
    path = os.path.join(data_dir, 'trending.txt')
    if os.path.exists(path):
        with open(path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
            for line in f:
                parts = line.strip().split('|')
                if len(parts) == 6:
                    trending.append({
                        'auction_id': int(parts[0]),
                        'item_name': parts[1],
                        'bid_count': int(parts[2]),
                        'current_bid': float(parts[3]),
                        'trending_rank': int(parts[4]),
                        'time_period': parts[5]
                    })
    return trending

# Save updated auctions (used for updating current_bid in place_bid POST)
def save_auctions(auctions):
    path = os.path.join(data_dir, 'auctions.txt')
    with open(path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
        for a in auctions:
            line = '|'.join([
                str(a['auction_id']),
                a['item_name'],
                a['description'],
                a['category'],
                f"{a['starting_bid']:.2f}",
                f"{a['current_bid']:.2f}",
                a['end_time'],
                a['status'],
                a['image_url']
            ])
            f.write(line + '\n')

# Save updated bids (append new bid)
def append_bid(bid):
    path = os.path.join(data_dir, 'bids.txt')
    with open(path, 'a', encoding='utf-8') as f:
        line = '|'.join([
            str(bid['bid_id']),
            str(bid['auction_id']),
            bid['bidder_name'],
            f"{bid['bid_amount']:.2f}",
            bid['bid_timestamp']
        ])
        f.write(line + '\n')

# Save updated bid history (append new history record)
def append_bid_history(history):
    path = os.path.join(data_dir, 'bid_history.txt')
    with open(path, 'a', encoding='utf-8') as f:
        line = '|'.join([
            str(history['history_id']),
            str(history['auction_id']),
            history['auction_name'],
            history['bidder_name'],
            f"{history['bid_amount']:.2f}",
            history['bid_timestamp']
        ])
        f.write(line + '\n')

# Utility to find next bid_id

def get_next_bid_id():
    bids = load_bids()
    max_id = 0
    for b in bids:
        if b['bid_id'] > max_id:
            max_id = b['bid_id']
    return max_id + 1

# Utility to find next history_id

def get_next_history_id():
    bid_hist = load_bid_history()
    max_id = 0
    for h in bid_hist:
        if h['history_id'] > max_id:
            max_id = h['history_id']
    return max_id + 1

@app.route('/')
def root_redirect():
    return redirect(url_for('dashboard_view'))

@app.route('/dashboard')
def dashboard_view():
    # Load auctions and trending
    auctions = load_auctions()
    trending = load_trending()

    # featured_auctions: list of dict{auction_id, item_name, current_bid}
    # Let's consider featured as first 3 active auctions or all if less
    featured_auctions = [
        {
            'auction_id': a['auction_id'],
            'item_name': a['item_name'],
            'current_bid': a['current_bid']
        }
        for a in auctions if a['status'] == 'Active'
    ]
    featured_auctions = featured_auctions[:3]

    # trending_auctions: list of dict{auction_id, item_name, current_bid, bid_count}
    trending_auctions = [
        {
            'auction_id': t['auction_id'],
            'item_name': t['item_name'],
            'current_bid': t['current_bid'],
            'bid_count': t['bid_count']
        }
        for t in trending
    ]

    return render_template('dashboard.html',
                           featured_auctions=featured_auctions,
                           trending_auctions=trending_auctions)

@app.route('/catalog')
def auction_catalog():
    auctions = load_auctions()
    categories = load_categories()

    # auctions: list of dict{auction_id, item_name, description, category, current_bid, end_time, image_url}
    auctions_out = []
    for a in auctions:
        auctions_out.append({
            'auction_id': a['auction_id'],
            'item_name': a['item_name'],
            'description': a['description'],
            'category': a['category'],
            'current_bid': a['current_bid'],
            'end_time': a['end_time'],
            'image_url': a['image_url']
        })

    # categories: list of dict{category_id, category_name}
    categories_out = [{'category_id': c['category_id'], 'category_name': c['category_name']} for c in categories]

    return render_template('catalog.html', auctions=auctions_out, categories=categories_out)

@app.route('/auction/<int:auction_id>')
def auction_details(auction_id):
    auctions = load_auctions()
    bid_history = load_bid_history()

    # Find auction by id
    auction = None
    for a in auctions:
        if a['auction_id'] == auction_id:
            auction = {
                'auction_id': a['auction_id'],
                'item_name': a['item_name'],
                'description': a['description'],
                'current_bid': a['current_bid'],
                'end_time': a['end_time'],
                'status': a['status']
            }
            break

    # bid_history filtered for this auction
    bid_history_filtered = [
        {'bidder_name': b['bidder_name'], 'bid_amount': b['bid_amount'], 'bid_timestamp': b['bid_timestamp']}
        for b in bid_history if b['auction_id'] == auction_id
    ]

    return render_template('auction_details.html', auction=auction, bid_history=bid_history_filtered)

@app.route('/auction/<int:auction_id>/place_bid', methods=['GET'])
def place_bid(auction_id):
    auctions = load_auctions()

    auction = None
    for a in auctions:
        if a['auction_id'] == auction_id:
            auction = {
                'auction_id': a['auction_id'],
                'item_name': a['item_name'],
                'minimum_bid': max(a['current_bid'], a['starting_bid']) + 0.01
            }
            break

    return render_template('place_bid.html', auction=auction)

@app.route('/auction/<int:auction_id>/place_bid', methods=['POST'])
def submit_bid(auction_id):
    auctions = load_auctions()
    error_message = None
    auction = None

    for a in auctions:
        if a['auction_id'] == auction_id:
            auction = {
                'auction_id': a['auction_id'],
                'item_name': a['item_name'],
                'minimum_bid': max(a['current_bid'], a['starting_bid']) + 0.01
            }
            break

    bidder_name = request.form.get('bidder-name', '').strip()
    bid_amount_str = request.form.get('bid-amount', '').strip()

    # Basic validation
    if not bidder_name:
        error_message = 'Bidder name is required.'
    try:
        bid_amount = float(bid_amount_str)
    except ValueError:
        error_message = 'Invalid bid amount.'
        bid_amount = None

    if auction is None:
        error_message = 'Auction not found.'

    if error_message is None and bid_amount is not None:
        min_bid = max(auction['minimum_bid'], 0)
        if bid_amount < min_bid:
            error_message = f'Bid must be at least {min_bid:.2f}.'

    if error_message:
        return render_template('place_bid.html', auction=auction, error_message=error_message)

    # Add bid record
    bids = load_bids()
    new_bid_id = get_next_bid_id()
    timestamp = datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M')

    new_bid = {
        'bid_id': new_bid_id,
        'auction_id': auction_id,
        'bidder_name': bidder_name,
        'bid_amount': bid_amount,
        'bid_timestamp': timestamp
    }
    append_bid(new_bid)

    # Add to bid history
    bid_histories = load_bid_history()
    new_history_id = get_next_history_id()
    auction_name = auction['item_name']
    new_history = {
        'history_id': new_history_id,
        'auction_id': auction_id,
        'auction_name': auction_name,
        'bidder_name': bidder_name,
        'bid_amount': bid_amount,
        'bid_timestamp': timestamp
    }
    append_bid_history(new_history)

    # Update current_bid in auctions
    for a in auctions:
        if a['auction_id'] == auction_id:
            a['current_bid'] = bid_amount
            break
    save_auctions(auctions)

    # Redirect to auction details
    return redirect(url_for('auction_details', auction_id=auction_id))

@app.route('/bids')
def bid_history_view():
    bids = load_bids()
    auctions = load_auctions()

    # bids: list of dict{bid_id, auction_name, bidder_name, bid_amount, bid_timestamp}
    # Need auction_name for bids
    auction_map = {a['auction_id']: a['item_name'] for a in auctions}
    bids_out = []
    for b in bids:
        auction_name = auction_map.get(b['auction_id'], 'Unknown Auction')
        bids_out.append({
            'bid_id': b['bid_id'],
            'auction_name': auction_name,
            'bidder_name': b['bidder_name'],
            'bid_amount': b['bid_amount'],
            'bid_timestamp': b['bid_timestamp']
        })

    # auctions: list of dict{auction_id, auction_name} for filter dropdown
    auctions_out = [{'auction_id': a['auction_id'], 'auction_name': a['item_name']} for a in auctions]

    return render_template('bid_history.html', bids=bids_out, auctions=auctions_out)

@app.route('/categories')
def categories_view():
    categories = load_categories()
    return render_template('categories.html', categories=categories)

@app.route('/winners')
def winners_view():
    winners_data = load_winners()
    winners_out = []
    for w in winners_data:
        winners_out.append({
            'auction_id': w['auction_id'],
            'item_name': w['item_name'],
            'winner_name': w['winner_name'],
            'winning_bid': w['winning_bid']
        })
    return render_template('winners.html', winners=winners_out)

@app.route('/trending')
def trending_auctions_view():
    trending = load_trending()
    trending_out = []
    for t in trending:
        trending_out.append({
            'auction_id': t['auction_id'],
            'item_name': t['item_name'],
            'bid_count': t['bid_count'],
            'current_bid': t['current_bid'],
            'trending_rank': t['trending_rank'],
            'time_period': t['time_period']
        })
    return render_template('trending.html', trending_auctions=trending_out)

@app.route('/status')
def auction_status_view():
    auctions = load_auctions()
    auctions_status = []
    for a in auctions:
        # Calculate time_remaining from end_time
        time_remaining = ''
        try:
            end_dt = datetime.strptime(a['end_time'], '%Y-%m-%d %H:%M')
            now = datetime.now()
            if end_dt > now:
                delta = end_dt - now
                days = delta.days
                hours = delta.seconds // 3600
                minutes = (delta.seconds % 3600) // 60
                time_remaining = f'{days}d {hours}h {minutes}m'
            else:
                time_remaining = 'Ended'
        except:
            time_remaining = 'Unknown'

        auctions_status.append({
            'auction_id': a['auction_id'],
            'item_name': a['item_name'],
            'status': a['status'],
            'time_remaining': time_remaining,
            'current_bid': a['current_bid']
        })

    return render_template('status.html', auctions_status=auctions_status)

if __name__ == '__main__':
    app.run(debug=True, port=5000)

required.'     try:         bid_amount = float(bid_amount_str)     except ValueError:         error_message = 'Invalid bid amount.'         bid_amount = None      if auction is None:         error_message = 'Auction not found.'      if error_message is None and bid_amount is not None:         min_bid = max(auction['minimum_bid'], 0)         if bid_amount < min_bid:             error_message = f'Bid must be at least {min_bid:.2f}.'      if error_message:         return render_template('place_bid.html', auction=auction, error_message=error_message)      # Add bid record     bids = load_bids()     new_bid_id = get_next_bid_id()     timestamp = datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M')      new_bid = {         'bid_id': new_bid_id,         'auction_id': auction_id,         'bidder_name': bidder_name,         'bid_amount': bid_amount,         'bid_timestamp': timestamp     }     append_bid(new_bid)      # Add to bid history     bid_histories = load_bid_history()     new_history_id = get_next_history_id()     auction_name = auction['item_name']     new_history = {         'history_id': new_history_id,         'auction_id': auction_id,         'auction_name': auction_name,         'bidder_name': bidder_name,         'bid_amount': bid_amount,         'bid_timestamp': timestamp     }     append_bid_history(new_history)      # Update current_bid in auctions     for a in auctions:         if a['auction_id'] == auction_id:             a['current_bid'] = bid_amount             break     save_auctions(auctions)      # Redirect to auction details     return auction_name, bidder_name, bid_amount, bid_timestamp}     # Need auction_name for bids     auction_map = {a['auction_id']: a['item_name'] for a in auctions}     bids_out = []     for b in bids:         auction_name = auction_map.get(b['auction_id'], 'Unknown Auction')         bids_out.append({             'bid_id': b['bid_id'],             'auction_name': auction_name,             'bidder_name': b['bidder_name'],             'bid_amount': b['bid_amount'],             'bid_timestamp': b['bid_timestamp']         })      # auctions: list of dict{auction_id, auction_name} for filter dropdown     auctions_out = [{'auction_id': a['auction_id'], 'auction_name': a['item_name']} for a in auctions]      return render_template('bid_history.html', bids=bids_out, auctions=auctions_out)  @app.route('/categories') def categories_view():     categories = load_categories()     return render_template('categories.html', categories=categories)  @app.route('/winners') def winners_view():     winners_data = load_winners()     winners_out = []     for w in winners_data:         winners_out.append({             'auction_id': w['auction_id'],             'item_name': w['item_name'],             'winner_name': w['winner_name'],             'winning_bid': w['winning_bid']         })     return render_template('winners.html', winners=winners_out)  @app.route('/trending') def trending_auctions_view():     trending = load_trending()     trending_out = []     for t in trending:         trending_out.append({             'auction_id': t['auction_id'],             'item_name': t['item_name'],             'bid_count': t['bid_count'],             'current_bid': t['current_bid'],             'trending_rank': t['trending_rank'],             'time_period': t['time_period']         })     return render_template('trending.html', trending_auctions=trending_out)  @app.route('/status') def auction_status_view():     auctions = load_auctions()     auctions_status = []     for a in auctions:         # Calculate time_remaining from end_time         time_remaining = ''         try:             end_dt = datetime.strptime(a['end_time'], '%Y-%m-%d %H:%M')             now = datetime.now()             if end_dt > now:                 delta = end_dt - now                 days = delta.days                 hours = delta.seconds // 3600                 minutes = (delta.seconds % 3600) // 60                 time_remaining = f'{days}d {hours}h {minutes}m'             else:                 time_remaining = 'Ended'         except:             time_remaining = 'Unknown'          auctions_status.append({             'auction_id': a['auction_id'],             'item_name': a['item_name'],             'status': a['status'],             'time_remaining': time_remaining,             'current_bid': a['current_bid']         })      return render_template('status.html', auctions_status=auctions_status)  if __name__ == '__main__':     app.run(debug=True, NEED_MODIFY

The provided app.py code contains multiple syntax errors and logical bugs that prevent it from running. Key issues include:

1. Incorrect imports:
 - 'form flask' instead of 'from flask'
 - misspelled import names (e.g., 'render_templat', 'requestt', 'redirectt', 'flsh')

2. Incorrect initialization:
 - 'app = flask(__name__)' instead of 'app = Flask(__name__)'
 - Incorrect secret_key assignment 'app.secret_key == ...' should be '='

3. File path errors:
 - joining paths incorrectly, e.g., os.path.join missing commas

4. File reading errors:
 - opening files in write mode ('w') instead of read mode ('r')
 - wrong encoding in users file (utf-16) inconsistent with others

5. Data parsing errors:
 - splitting lines incorrectly (e.g., line.strip.split instead of line.strip().split)
 - wrong number of parts expected in splits
 - inconsistent indices for file parts
 - returning a single 'item' or 'bid' instead of the list

6. Logical errors:
 - returning empty lists early instead of processing files
 - incorrect conditional checks like 'if os.path.exists(ITEMS_FILE): return []' meaning if file exists, we return empty
 - comparing variables incorrectly (e.g., 'is' instead of '==')
 - wrong method parameters (e.g., methods='POST', string instead of list)
 - wrong or missing parameters in redirects and url_for
 - assigning variables wrong or missing colons
 - missing commas in dict definitions

7. Other issues:
 - sorting bids ascending instead of descending
 - missing error handling
 - app running multiple times with repeated if __name__ == '__main__'

In conclusion, the code needs significant fixes as mentioned above to run properly and support backend functionalities.

Once corrected, thorough backend tests should be applied to verify:
- Data loading correctness from files
- Flask route responses and rendering
- Business logic for bids and items
- Error handling and edge cases

RECOMMENDATION: Fix app.py according to the above points before retesting.
